<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:духовой.html>духово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">duxovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wind; brass
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:духовой.html>духово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:инструмент.html>инструме́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>duxovój</b> instrumént</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>wind</b> instrument</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:духовой.html>духово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оркестр.html>орке́стр</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>duxovój</b> orkéstr</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>brass</b> band</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>heat-operated</li>
<li>pneumatic</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:духота.html>духота́</a> (10645)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:духота.html>духота́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">duxotá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:духота.html>духоты́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>sultriness, closeness, stuffiness, sultry / stuffy air</li></ol>

<ol><li>рассекатель</li>
<li>—</li>

***душа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душа</a> (236)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">доуша</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">duša</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soul</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*duša</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душа́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dušá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>души́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́ши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душ</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>soul
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>души́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ot <b>duší</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from the heart</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душа</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нараспашку.html>нараспа́шку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>duša</b> naraspášku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">frank-hearted, heart on one's sleeve</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глубина.html>глубине́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>души́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v glubiné <b>duší</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">deep in one's heart</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bratʹ zá <b>dušu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">touch the heart</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душа</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>duša</b> v <b>dúšu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in perfect harmony/concord</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душа́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сте</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dušá</b> ne na méste</i> ― <span class="e-translation">anxious, worried</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душе́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne po <b>dušé</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">displeases</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душе́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>dušé</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">pleasant</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душо́й</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stojátʹ nad <b>dušój</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pester/harass/plague smb.</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залезать.html>залеза́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></b> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zalezátʹ v <b>dúšu</b> komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to worm oneself into smb.'s confidence</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душо́й</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>dušój</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">with spirit/feeling/zeal</span></div></dd>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:душевный.html>душе́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dušévnyj</span>)

<ol><li>mental, psychic</li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">душе-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">duše-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздирающий.html>раздира́ющий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razdirájuščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:душераздирающий.html>душераздира́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dušerazdirájuščij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>heartbreaking, heartrending</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> deliberately tragic</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:душивший.html>души́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dušívšij</span>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:душить.html>души́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dušítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***душить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:душить.html>души́ть</a> (6499)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dušiti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:душить.html>души́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dušítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задушить.html>задуши́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to smother, to stifle, to strangle, to throttle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:душить.html>души́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:объятие.html>объя́тиях</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dušítʹ</b> v obʺjátijax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to press to one's bosom, to embrace warmly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to oppress, to stifle, to repress, to suppress</li>
<li>to choke, to suffocate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злоба.html>зло́ба</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душить.html>ду́шит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zlóba <b>dúšit</b> jevó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is choking with anger</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">

***дыбом.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дыбом.html>ды́бом</a> (14616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Apparently the instrumental case of a no-longer-existent word; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дыба.html>дыбы́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na dybý</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on its hind legs <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a horse</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ом</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-om</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дыбом.html>ды́бом</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dýbom</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>(standing) on end
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>вста́ли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дыбом.html>ды́бом</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó vólosy vstáli <b>dýbom</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his hair stood on end</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дым.html>дым</a> (943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dymъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰuh₂mós</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">smoke</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***дымка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дымок.html>дымка</a> (18282)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дым.html>дым</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dym</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">smoke, fume</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дымок.html>ды́мка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dýmka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дымок.html>ды́мки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дымок.html>ды́мки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дымок.html>ды́мок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>haze, gauze, mist</li></ol>

***дымок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дымок.html>дымок</a> (4525)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дым.html>дым</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dym</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дымок.html>дымо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dymók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дымок.html>дымка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дымок.html>дымки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дымок.html>дымко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>small stream of smoke
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><b>1863</b>, Л. Н. <a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>То́лстой</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>Казаки</a></i> :<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдруг.html>Вдруг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:показаться.html>показа́лся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дымок.html>дымок</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оттуда.html>отту́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:свистнуть.html>сви́стнула</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пулька.html>пу́лька</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vdrug pokazálsja <b>dymok</b> ottúda, svístnula ješčó pulʹka.</i></dd></dl><ul><li><b>1911</b> translation by Louise and Aylmer Maude<dl><dd>Suddenly a little cloud of smoke appeared from thence, and again a bullet whistled past.</dd></dl></li></ul></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дыра.html>дыра́</a> (3316)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дыра.html>дыра́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dyrá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дыра.html>дыры́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дыра.html>ды́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дыра.html>ды́р</a></b>)
